<table>

<tr>
<th>Incipit
</th>
<td>1. (Cello Solo)<img src="/images/lilypond/1167566095c0f014fc6a1d8fab320c18.png" alt="\relative c'&#10;{&#10;\version &quot;2.18.0&quot;&#10;\key b \minor&#9;&#10;\time 4/4&#10;\clef bass&#10;\tempo &quot;Allegro. Quasi improvisando&quot;&#10;b4. _\markup{\dynamic f \italic&quot; risoluto&quot; } \downbow cis16 dis b2 \upbow | &#10;b4. \downbow a16 fis b2 \upbow | &#10;b8._\&lt; dis16 fis8.-> e16 dis4->\! &lt; a, fis' c' >->\fz \arpeggio | &#10;&lt; fis dis' b' >^>\fz \arpeggio &lt; fis dis' a' >^>\fz \arpeggio &lt; es c' g' >^>\fz \arpeggio &lt;dis a' fis'>^>\fz \arpeggio |&#10;}&#10;" />
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Cello Concerto
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Koncert pro violoncello a orchestr
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.104&#160;; B.191
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 11
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>B minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 movements:
<ol><li> Allegro (B minor)
</li><li> Adagio ma non troppo (G major)
</li><li> Finale. Allegro moderato (B minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1894–95
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1896-03-19 in London
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1896
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Hanuš Wihan (1855–1920)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>39 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Solo:</i> cello<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes (2nd also piccolo), 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons,<br />3 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones, tuba, timpani, triangle, strings
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cello_Concerto_(Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cello Concerto (Dvořák)">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.antonin-dvorak.cz/en/concerto-for-cello2">antonin-dvorak.cz</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History:
<ul><li> Composed for cello and orchestra, 1894–95 (= B.191)
</li><li> Arranged for cello and piano by Dvořák, 1894–95 (= B.522)
</li><li> Discrepancies in the various editions:
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li> 1st Movement, Measure 90, Cello Solo part
</li></ul>
